<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size: 14pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri Light&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc485150867"><span lang="EN-GB">Chapter 1: Before you start</span></a></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150868"><span lang="EN-GB">Is openHAB2 the right choice for
my home automation project?</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Be aware that openHAB2 is an OPEN home
automation solution which is strongly living from a very supportive community.
If you want to have a plug and play solution with supplier guaranteed service
level and a high likeliness that all the features are working and all the
hardware is compatible, you might be better off in getting a ready to use home
automation kit including the designated controller (like e.g. devolo or
homematic IP). Consider this especially if you are planning to do safety
related automation or emergency detection like fire alarm. </span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">If you, on the other hand, are willing to
spend a few hrs/days in learning how to do a little installation and coding
yourself and have no problems with the service level of a Raspberry Pi 3 (it is
not as failsafe as other controllers) you might find a perfect environment with
openHAB2 for your low cost, very flexible and continuously improving home
automation environment.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150869"><span lang="EN-GB">Introduction:</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">This tutorial is targeting beginners like
me to get a step by step guideline to get all the things installed. Since I am
no coding expert and have no experience in Raspberry and Raspbian I am trying
to go through the things step by step, so you should be able to get everything
done, even without exactly having to go into all the details. That is one of
the reasons I am also using the graphical GUI PIXEL for Raspbian since I thing
it makes it easier for the beginners to get started (and you might want to use
PIXEL anyway when you are using the Raspberry 7” display as interface for your
home automation controller)</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">This tutorial is also based on <b>having a Windows
PC</b> to support the setup process. You might be able to completely do it
without the support of an extra PC, if you can get a MicroSD card with a
pre-installed Raspbian OS and use the display options (the Raspberry 7” display
or HDMI Display) for the Raspberry.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="color: red;" lang="EN-GB">DISCLAIMER:</span></b></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><i><span style="color: red;" lang="EN-GB">This tutorial might
contain some typos, errors or ways of setting up, which can be done in a better
way. I am just reflecting my process of starting from scratch and slowly
working my way through hundreds of online tutorials, manuals, forum threads
etc. and on the way, highlighting the issues I had in getting things working.
There will be no guarantee that the given instructions are working for your
project as well.</span></i></b></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Anyway I hope this tutorial will help some
beginners to enjoy home automation with openHAB2.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150870"><span lang="EN-GB">A few words about the 2 in
openHAB2:</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">The 2 in openHAB2 is important! The
tutorial is based on the openHAB2 and will not go into all the details of the
old version.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">You just have to be aware, that a lot of
online documentation is still for the openHAB version and will <b>not</b> be
applicable for openHAB2!</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">So the best thing is always to go to the
official webpage of openHAB2 and start from there, and only if you really can’t
find the information or the link there, go to google and search for other
solutions. I was always using the search setting (last year) so it was more
likely to the results considering openHAB2 and not openHAB.<br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc485150871"><span lang="EN-GB">Chapter 2: Preparation</span></a></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150872"><span lang="EN-GB">Shopping list:</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">As mentioned before, I am basing this
tutorial on the graphical GUI of Raspbian named PIXEL so the shopping list is
also containing parts for this optional setup:</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150873"><span lang="EN-GB">Minimal setup of the controller:</span></a></h3>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 6" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image002.jpg" alt="Product Details" height="147" width="218"></p>

 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Designated Raspberry power supply (min. 2,5A 5V, I recommend
  3A) <i>Do not use other USB chargers since insufficient power supply (shown
  in GUI as lightening symbol in the upper right corner) will result in serious
  issues like e.g. Bluetooth not working</i>) A cable switch might be a good
  thing since you might have to hard-reset your Pi in the early days more often
  and the Pi itself does not have a power switch</span></p>

  </td>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150875"><span lang="EN-GB">Z-Wave Controller</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">If you want to use the Z-Wave technology
for your home automation project you have to have one Z-Wave controller
connected to your Raspberry</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE</span></b><span lang="EN-GB">: Be
aware that the details serial numbers or item names may vary since you have to
always make sure to use the hardware which is allowed in your country!</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Aeotec by Aeon Labs Z-Stick Gen5</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Pros:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">Allows offline inclusion of Z-Wave devices
  which makes it very easy since you only have to take the stick to the mounted
  device, not the entire Raspberry</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Cons:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">Including battery powered devices into openHAB2
  requires a special process (see tutorial)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 18" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image018.jpg" alt="Product Details" height="108" width="108"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><i><span lang="EN-GB">Alternative</span></i><span lang="EN-GB">: UZB
  Z-Wave PLUS USB stick by Z-Wave.Me </span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Pros:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">Cheapest controller</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Cons:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">For inclusion, the controller has to be
  plugged into the Raspberry, so for mounted devices like wall switches , you
  have to take the Raspberry in close proximity of the device or do the
  inclusion before you mount the switch inside the wall</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">

  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><i><span lang="EN-GB">NOT REALLY an Alternative</span></i><span lang="EN-GB">: RaZberry2 Z-Wave Plus Daughter Card for Raspberry Pi Home
  Automation <i>(not plug and play compatible with optional setup of the
  controller with 7” Raspberry display!)</i></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Pros:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">will be mounted directly on the Raspberry so
  it is not using a USB port</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Cons:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">will be mounted directly on the Raspberry which
  is blocking the GPIO pins for e.g. the Display power supply or additional
  cooling fans, so you have to manually solder the power wires at the back of
  the razberry</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">is using the i/o port of the Raspberry Pi 3 on
  board Bluetooth, so a lot of additional configuration is needed to get the
  razberry and the Bluetooth running in parallel.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">most expensive controller</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="position: absolute; z-index: 251636736; margin-left: 47px; margin-top: 12px; width: 95px; height: 86px;"><img src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image020.png" height="86" width="95"></span><img id="Picture 20" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image021.jpg" alt="Product Details" height="101" width="153"></p>
  </td>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150876"><span lang="EN-GB">Z-Wave sensors, switches and
actuators</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE</span></b><span lang="EN-GB">: Be
aware that the details serial numbers or item names may vary since you have to
always make sure to use the hardware which is allowed in your country!</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Since I am doing a German based home
automation project you may find that some Z-Wave devices are not sold in your
required country configuration ( e.g. Z-Wave NodOn Smart Plug not available
e.g. in the US)</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Z-Wave Fibaro Double Switch 2, Z-Wave Plus Smart
  Switch (comes at almost the same costs than the single switch and gives you 2
  channels. Only reason to go for single switch is you need the full power
  range of the single switch since the double switch has slightly lower range)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: This switch is designed to be installed in the
  electrical power wiring of your home (inside a distributor case). In some
  countries this may only be allowed to be done by special trained staff
  (insurance and/or law). </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">

  US)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 25" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image025.jpg" alt="Z-Wave NodOn Smart Plug, Schalt- und Messsteckdose, Schuko, 1 Stück, NODEMSP3101" height="87" width="87"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> if you
want to by other Z-Wave devices always make your they are listed in the Z-Wave
device list of the openHAB2 Z-Wave binding to make sure they are supported
correctly in the context of openHAB2:</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><a href="http://www.cd-jackson.com/index.php/zwave/zwave-device-database/zwave-device-list"><span class="Heading9Char"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; color: windowtext; text-decoration: none;" lang="EN-GB">http://www.cd-jackson.com/index.php/zwave/zwave-device-database/zwave-device-list</span></span></a></p>

<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150877"><span lang="EN-GB">LAN devices (cable or WiFi)</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">A lot of things you are using at home are
already connected to your LAN and can be integrated into your openHAB2 home
automation project if the right binding is available for that device.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">You can find an overview on </span><a href="http://docs.openhab.org/addons/bindings.html"><span class="Heading9Char"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; color: windowtext; text-decoration: none;" lang="EN-GB">http://docs.openhab.org/addons/bindings.html</span></span></a></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE</span></b><span lang="EN-GB">: Be
aware that not all the bindings to include devices are already included in the
stable version of openHAB2 and may require a manual installation of a so called
snapshot version of the binding (how to install snapshot bindings is explained
later in this tutorial since we will need it for the WiFi LED controller)</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">WiFi XCSOURCE Magic UFO-WiFi LED-Controller Type
  LD382 (other brand names might work as well, but you have to make sure it is
  Type LD382, LD382A or LD686)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">REMARK: I was using a WiFi controller on purpose
  since:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">it is only about half the price of a Z-Wave
  WiFi controller</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">you can control the device as well via smart
  phone (like light to music feature of the app)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">But some things you have to be aware of using WiFi
  LED instead of Z-Wave LED:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">you have to have a WiFi network to which your
  Raspberry and your WiFi LED controller is connected</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-<span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span><span lang="EN-GB">you have to manually install a beta / snapshot
  version of openHAB2 or manually install the WiFi LED Binding on top of the
  package based installation of openHAB2 (see tutorial)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 97" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image026.jpg" alt="Product Details" border="0" height="91" width="91"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">RGB LED stripe incl. power supply 12V DC bundle</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">While you can buy the stripe and the power supply
  bundle separately, most of the times the bundle will come at the same price
  or even cheaper. The included power supply plug should directly fit into the
  power inlet socket of the WiFi controller.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">REMARK: It also allows you to attach the stripe
  without soldering since you can just cut the cable of the RGB bundle
  controller and use it to connect the LED stripe to the WiFi controller.</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 197" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image027.jpg" alt="LE 5m 150 5050 Leds Flexibler LED Streifen, RGB, Farbwechsel, DIY-Beleuchtung led strip Inklusive Netzteil und 44 Tasten IR-Fernbedienung, LED Lichtband, Deko, Weihnachten, Party, Ambientbeleuchtung" border="0" height="137" width="137"><img id="Picture 196" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image028.jpg" alt="Product Details" border="0" height="143" width="143"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Since the WiFi LED-Controller is allowing you to at

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

PCs as well, but you have to go online to look up the differences and do some
adaptions on the tutorial e.g. mounting the Raspberry file system to PC)</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150880"><span lang="EN-GB">Raspberry downloads:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">How to download software will be explained
in the tutorial, but as a reference you will use</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">openHAB2</span></b><span lang="EN-GB">
Package repository based installation or manual installation (be aware that the
file locations on the Raspberry will be different based on which kind of
installation you choose)</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">Samba</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> server(for
access of Raspberry files from Windows machine; needed for Eclipse Smart HomeDesigner)</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">xscreensaver</span></b><span lang="EN-GB">
(optional if you are using the display setup, to easy control screen blackening
or screen savers)</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Lucida Bright&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Lucida Bright&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Lucida Bright&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc485150881"><span lang="EN-GB">Chapter 3: Raspberry hardware and Raspbian
OS installation</span></a></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150882"><span lang="EN-GB">General information about Raspberry
interfaces and GPIO pins:</span></a></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150883"><span lang="EN-GB">Raspberry input Overview:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><img id="Picture 40" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image032.jpg" alt="Bildergebnis für raspberry pi 3" border="0" height="406" width="642"></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150884"><span lang="EN-GB">Raspberry GPIO pin Overview:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><img id="Picture 41" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image033.png" alt="Bildergebnis für raspberry pi 3 gpio" border="0" height="383" width="642"></p>

<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150885"><span lang="EN-GB">Preparing MicroSD card - writing Raspbian
image to MicroSD card (PC required):</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 236.65pt;" valign="top" width="316">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 10pt; line-height: 115%;"><span lang="EN-GB">Download latest Raspbian Release (*.zip file) to a Windows folder</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 256.05pt;" valign="top" width="341">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 10pt; line-height: 115%;"><img id="Picture 29" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image034.jpg" border="0" height="154" width="327"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 236.65pt;" valign="top" width="316">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 10pt; line-height: 115%;"><span lang="EN-GB">Extract *.zip file to receive *.img file</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 256.05pt;" valign="top" width="341">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 10pt; line-height: 115%;"><img id="Picture 58" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image035.jpg" border="0" height="224" width="302"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 236.65pt;" valign="top" width="316">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 10pt; line-height: 115%;"><span lang="EN-GB">Use Etcher to write image to a MicroSD card</span></p>
  <ol style="margin-top: 0cm;" start="1" type="1">
   <li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">select image</span></li>
   <li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">select drive with MicroSD card
       plugged in to</span></li>
   <li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">start flashing</span></li>
  </ol>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 256.05pt;" valign="top" width="341">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 10pt; line-height: 115%;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;"><img id="Picture 42" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image036.jpg" border="0" height="164" width="320"></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150888"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: Installation of 7” Raspberry
display and display case:</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">The full tutorial will be found on:</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><a href="https://www.element14.com/community/docs/DOC-78156/l/raspberry-pi-7-touchscreen-display"><span class="Heading9Char"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; color: windowtext; text-decoration: none;" lang="EN-GB">https://www.element14.com/community/docs/DOC-78156/l/Raspberry-pi-7-touchscreen-display</span></span></a></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">and a clip on YouTube:</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tK-w-wDvRTg"><span class="Heading9Char"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; color: windowtext; text-decoration: none;" lang="EN-GB">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tK-w-wDvRTg</span></span></a></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">Remark</span></b><span lang="EN-GB">: I
had an issue with plugging in the power supply to the micro USB power input on
the circuit board of the display (like shown in the video). The Raspberry was
still showing me the low power symbol (lightening symbol on the upper right
corner) SOLUTION:&nbsp; I had to plug in the power supply to the micro USB power
input on the Raspberry itself. The display is now powered via the jumper
cables. The standard display case is also allowing for both micro USB power
inputs to be used.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE</span></b><span lang="EN-GB">: If the
image on the display is having the wrong orientation, you can rotate the image
by changing the configuration of Raspbian (see tutorial section Initial
configuration of Raspbian)</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc485150890"><span lang="EN-GB">Chapter 4: Raspbian basic configuration</span></a></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150891"><span lang="EN-GB">Starting up Raspberry or the first
time – Raspbian PIXEL desktop</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Since this tutorial is focussing on using
the PIXEL GUI here are a few basic tips</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Raspberry start-up screen</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><img id="Picture 60" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image054.jpg" border="0" height="184" width="245"></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">PIXEL basic desktop (including the programs
used in this tutorial) not unlike other PC OS desktops:</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="position: absolute; z-index: 251685888; margin-left: 346px; margin-top: 19px; width: 152px; height: 167px;"><img src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image055.png" alt="network configuration" height="167" width="152"></span><span style="position: absolute; z-index: 251677696; margin-left: 281px; margin-top: 14px; width: 197px; height: 108px;"><img src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image056.png" alt="Bluetooth configuration" height="108" width="197"></span><span style="position: absolute; z-index: 251669504; margin-left: 77px; margin-top: 13px; width: 158px; height: 100px;"><img src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image057.png" alt="Terminal" height="100" width="158"></span><span style="position: absolute; z-index: 251644928; margin-left: 12px; margin-top: 14px; width: 254px; height: 292px;"><img src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image058.png" alt="Applications menu (incl. access to configuration)" height="292" width="254"></span><span style="position: absolute; z-index: 251661312; margin-left: 56px; margin-top: 14px; width: 96px; height: 175px;"><img src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image059.png" alt="File manager" height="175" width="96"></span><span style="position: absolute; z-index: 251653120; margin-left: 27px; margin-top: 14px; width: 118px; height: 230px;"><img src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image060.png" alt="Web browser" height="230" width="118"></span><img id="Picture 61" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image061.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="315" width="597"></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: </span></b><span lang="EN-GB">If you
are working with the 7” Raspberry display setup you might need to flip/rotate
the display orientation. Just check the section” Optional: Change display
orientation” later in this chapter</span></p>

<b><span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span></b>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150892"><span lang="EN-GB">Working with the Terminal:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><img id="Picture 71" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image062.jpg" alt="newdesk" border="0" height="159" width="244"></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> As
soon as you have connected the Raspberry to the network you might find it
easier to open the Terminal remotely using PuTTY. This also allows you to
directly paste command lines from this tutorial into the Terminal. (Right click
in PuTTY terminal is pasting the content of the clipboard into the terminal)</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150893"><span lang="EN-GB">Basic terminal commands and functions:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">The full list can be found on:</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><a href="https://www.raspberrypi.org/documentation/linux/usage/commands.md"><span class="Heading9Char"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; color: windowtext; text-decoration: none;" lang="EN-GB">https://www.Raspberrypi.org/documentation/linux/usage/commands.md</span></span></a></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 154.25pt;" valign="top" width="206">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">help</p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 338.45pt;" valign="top" width="451">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Is showing you basic commands</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 154.25pt;" valign="top" width="206">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo <i>othercommand</i></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 338.45pt;" valign="top" width="451">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">is allowing you to run other commands as super user
  aka root user</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 154.25pt;" valign="top" width="206">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">ls -la</p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 338.45pt;" valign="top" width="451">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Shows the files in a directory incl. additional
  information</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 154.25pt;" valign="top" width="206">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">cd</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">cd</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">cd ..</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">cd <i>directory</i></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><i><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></i></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><i><span lang="EN-US">cd /directory/directory</span></i></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 338.45pt;" valign="top" width="451">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Is changing the shell working directory.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">It can be used with attributes:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">No attribute =&gt; working directory is changed to
  user root directory.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">working directory is changed to directory one level
  above</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">working directory is changed to the named </span><i><span lang="EN-US">directory</span></i><span lang="EN-GB"> inside the current directory</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">working directory is changed to the directory
  defined by the full path </span><i><span lang="EN-US">/directory/directory</span></i></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">.</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 154.25pt;" valign="top" width="206">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">nano <i>filename</i></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">(sudo nano<i> filename)</i></span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 338.45pt;" valign="top" width="451">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Is stating a basic editor in the terminal to open or
  create a simple text or configuration file, mostly you have to add a </span><span lang="EN-US">sudo</span><span lang="EN-GB"> if you want to be able to write the
  files with root user rights. Closing the editor is done by ctrl+x and then
  choosing whether you want to save your changes or not</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;" lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150894"><span lang="EN-GB">Initial configuration of Raspbian</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">The following steps make sure, that basic Raspbian
configuration is done. </span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> There
may be many tutorials in how to set-up and configure Raspbian and going into
more details about user rights and other Raspbian features. This tutorial is
showing the way which worked for my project aiming to run openHAB2 on the Raspberry.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Since this tutorial is using the PIXEL GUI
I always refer to the PIXEL way of configuring and only go back to the terminal
way (text only) if it is required.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150895"><span lang="EN-GB">Localisation:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">The 1.st thing you want to do is changing
the localisation settings to make sure your keyboard layout and WiFi settings
are matching.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> Do not
change the password before you have changed the keyboard layout since you might
put in a different password than you expect (e.g. US qwerty vs. German qwertz
results in “Raspberrz” instead of “Raspberry”)</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Raspberry Pi Configuration</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Application menu</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-Preferences</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">--Raspberry Pi configuration</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Go to tab Localisation</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150896"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: Change display
orientation</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">If you are working with the 7” Raspberry
display setup you might need to flip/rotate the display orientation for
specific cases</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 126" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image069.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 127" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image070.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open boot config.txt file in nano editor</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo nano /boot/config.txt</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Add the line at the bottom of the file:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">(This will flip the display orientation)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">lcd_rotate=2</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: You can choose from different angles</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 0 degrees rotation</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp; 90 degrees rotation</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">180 degrees rotation</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">270 degrees rotation</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">horizontal flip</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">vertical flip</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">display_rotate=0</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">display_rotate=1</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">display_rotate=2</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">display_rotate=3</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">display_rotate=0x10000</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">display_rotate=0x20000</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Exit and save the file </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;ctrl+x&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;y&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Enter&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Reboot the Raspberry for the changes to take effect</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo reboot</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150897"><span lang="EN-GB">Changing Password:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">This is important to secure your standard Raspberry
user “pi” before you connect the Raspberry to the network.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> Make
sure you have changed the keyboard layout to your requirements before change
the password.</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150900"><span lang="EN-GB">Check the IP address of the Raspberry:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">To do so you have to check the IP address
of the Raspberry in the terminal</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Start terminal by clicking on the icon</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 78" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image075.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="39" width="45"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">use the command</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">ifconfig</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Result: the terminal shows you the ip configuration
  and the IP addresses for the different connections</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Ethernet cable: </span><span lang="EN-US">eth0 <i>xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx</i></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">WiFi: </span><span lang="EN-US">wlan0 <i>xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx</i></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> You
might want to set your IP address of the Raspberry to static, if you get
problems with the lease time setting of your gateway (IP address is changing
whenever you reconnect to the network)</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150901"><span lang="EN-GB">Update / Upgrade Raspbian:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Raspbian is proving online updates so make
sure that you have the latest installed before you go further in the
configuration.</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Start terminal by clicking on the icon</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 80" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image075.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="39" width="45"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style="height: 56.6pt;">
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt; height: 56.6pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">use the command</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">(be aware that the upgrade function will take several
  minutes to complete if you run it for the first time)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt; height: 56.6pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo apt-get update</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo apt-get upgrade</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<b><span style="font-size: 13pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri Light&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span></b>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150902"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional Raspberry settings and
configuration:</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">The following settings and configuration is
just for additional information and might not be needed to setup openHAB2. Some
of the settings and configuration might still be useful.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150903"><span lang="EN-GB">Check partition size on MicroSD
card:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Make sure Raspbian is using the full
capacity of the MicroSD card (normally while starting up Raspbian for the first
time, it is done automatically and the Raspberry will restart automatically):</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 114" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image076.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 115" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image077.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">use the command</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo fdisk -l</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Result: the terminal shows you the partition size of
  the two partitions on the MicroSD card summing up to the total capacity </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Example for 16 GB:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">If the capacity is not completely used (e.g. you
  were using not a plain Raspbian image) you have to expand the partitions
  manually in the terminal configuration </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Start terminal configuration with command</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo raspi-config</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Select Option (Be aware that the option numbers
  might change in newer Raspbian releases)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">7 Advanced Options</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Select Option</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 292.1pt;" valign="top" width="389">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">A1 Expand Filesystem </span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Prompt will tell you that the file system has been
  increased</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 196.8pt;" valign="top" width="262">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now select to exit the configuration</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Yes&gt;</p>
  </td>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150904"><span lang="EN-GB">Create a Desktop icon and link it
to a application</span></a><span lang="EN-GB"> </span></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">To be able to create a Icon you have to
first create a *.desktop file</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> This
example is creating the desktop icon for the user “pi”</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 122" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image078.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 123" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image079.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Go to the directory desktop for your “pi” user</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">

  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Create a specific desktop file using nano editor</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo nano <i>yourdesktopfile</i>.desktop</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Enter parameters into the file accordingly</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Name: </span><i><span lang="EN-US">YourShortcutName</span></i></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Comment: </span><i><span lang="EN-US">Your Shortcut
  Comment</span></i></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Icon: </span><i><span lang="EN-US">YourIcon</span></i><span lang="EN-US">.png</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Application for shortcut: </span><span lang="EN-US">YourShortcutApp</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Desktop Entry]</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Name=<i>YourShortcutName</i></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Comment=<i>Your Shortcut Comment</i></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Icon=/usr/share/pixmaps/<i>YourIcon</i>.png</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Exec=/usr/bin/<i>YourShortcutApp</i></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Type=Application</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">Encoding=UTF-8</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">Terminal=false</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Exit and save the file </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;ctrl+x&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;y&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Enter&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
