<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri Light&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150905"><span lang="EN-GB">Enabling root user:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">Since by default the “root” disabled it
can’t be used. You might want to enable it for certain purposes like e.g.
enabling the root user for samba file server to get full access to the
directories from a PC (see chapter setup samba server) </span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> There
is a reason for the “root” being disabled! Enabling the user is allowing full
access to the Raspbian and therefore creating a security risk. Please always
consider whether you really want to enable this user!</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 109" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image076.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 79" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image080.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Since the user already exists you just have to set
  the password</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: you can also use the command to change the
  password later on</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo passwd root</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Just enter twice the new password for the “root”
  user</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><i>rootpassword</i></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><i>rootpassword</i> </p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150906"><span lang="EN-GB">Enabling remote SSH access for
root user:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> There
is a reason for the “root” not being enabled for SSH! Enabling the user for SSH
is allowing full remote access to the Raspbian and therefore creating a
significant security risk. Please always consider whether you really want to
enable this user for SSH!</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 110" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image078.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 82" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image081.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open sshd.config file in nano editor</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo nano /etc/ssh/sshd_config</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Find the section </span><span lang="EN-US">#
  Authentication</span><span lang="EN-GB"> in the file</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"># Authentication:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">LoginGraceTime 120</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">PermitRootLogin without-password</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">StrictModes yes</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">And change the </span><span lang="EN-US">PermitRootLoing</span><span lang="EN-GB"> line to</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">PermitRootLogin yes</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Exit and save the file </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;ctrl+x&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;y&gt;</p>

<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-size: 13pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri Light&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150907"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: Raspbian PIXEL
screensaver (xscreensaver)</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">If you are working with the 7” Raspberry
display setup you might want to use a screensaver as well.</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150908"><span lang="EN-GB">Installation of xscreensaver:</span></a></h3>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 111" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image076.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 94" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image080.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Install xscreensaver and some additional screen
  saver themes</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo apt-get install xscreensaver xscreensaver-data-extra
  xscreensaver-gl-extra</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;y&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150909"><span lang="EN-GB">Configuration of xscreensaver:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">I am showing an example configuration which
is first switching on a screensaver and then turning off the display
completely.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150910"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: Start Chromium Web
server on Raspbian boot</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150911"><span lang="EN-GB">Configure the autostart file:</span></a></h3>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 116" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image076.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 117" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image080.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open the autostart configuration file with nano
  editor</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo nano /home/pi/.config/lxsession/LXDE-pi/autostart</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Add the lines at the end of the file (ignoring error
  dialogs)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">@unclutter</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">@chromium-browser --noerrdialogs</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional parameters:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">--kiosk (for full screen mode. NOTE: to exit full
  screen mode you have to press “Alt+F4” on the keyboard of the Raspberry, so
  you have to have a keyboard installed to exit this mode!)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">--incognito (for incognito mode of the browser)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">http://yoururl.com (for selecting the URL directly
  in the configuration file. NOTE: selecting the URL via Chromium settings
  might be easier)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">@chromium-browser --noerrdialogs --kiosk --incognito
  http://<i>yoururl.com</i></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Exit and save the file </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;ctrl+x&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;y&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Enter&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Check if the browser is coming up after reboot</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo reboot</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150912"><span lang="EN-GB">Select the start URL for Chromium
web browser:</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: You can also select the URL in the
autostart file, but using the browser functionality is giving you a simpler
access (no terminal) and you can check the result without rebooting</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 243.3pt;" valign="top" width="324">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Chromium and go to the Settings</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">(3 bullets icon)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 249.4pt;" valign="top" width="333">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 118" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image085.jpg" border="0" height="232" width="316"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 243.3pt;" valign="top" width="324">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Select in the On start-up chapter the option</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&lt;check&gt;</span><span lang="EN-GB"> Open a
  specific page or set of pages</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">And click on the link </span><span lang="EN-US">&lt;Set
  pages&gt;</span><span lang="EN-GB"> to enter the requested start URL</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 249.4pt;" valign="top" width="333">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 119" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image086.jpg" border="0" height="230" width="318"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 243.3pt;" valign="top" width="324">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Enter the requested start URL </span><i><span lang="EN-US">http://yoururl.com</span></i></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&lt;OK&gt;</span><span lang="EN-GB"> your URL</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now Chromium is allowing you to enter an additional
  URL which you can ignore</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 249.4pt;" valign="top" width="333">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 120" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image087.jpg" border="0" height="227" width="315"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 243.3pt;" valign="top" width="324">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">To check if it is working</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Close Chromium browser</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Chromium browser</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Result: </span><i><span lang="EN-US">http://yoururl.com
  </span></i><span lang="EN-GB">should be loaded on startup (in my example I
  selected the openHAB2 GUI start page )</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: If you have completed your openHAB2

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">or even start specific pages in the HABPANEL GUI
  (just use the URL shown in the browser when you access the HABPANEL page)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 249.4pt;" valign="top" width="333">

<h1><a name="_Toc485150913"><span lang="EN-GB">Chapter 5: Setting up Raspbian for
access via PC</span></a></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150914"><span lang="EN-GB">Connect to the Raspberry terminal
your windows system using, KiTTY or PuTTY:</span></a></h2>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open KiTTY or PuTTY on your PC</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 81" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image089.jpg" border="0" height="274" width="283"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Enter Hostname (pi@ in front of the IP is giving the
  user you want to use for connecting, in this case the standard user “pi”),
  Port and Connection type</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Select Open to launch the terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 88" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image090.jpg" border="0" height="275" width="282"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Hostname: pi@<i>xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx</i></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Port:22</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Connection type: SSH</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Open&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional save the session</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 87" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image091.jpg" border="0" height="266" width="276"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Saved session </span><i>yoursessionname</i></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Save&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">On first connection an security alert is coming
  which you have to accept</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 83" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image092.jpg" border="0" height="180" width="265"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">Yes</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now a terminal window is opening on our PC asking
  you to enter the “pi” user password</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 84" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image093.jpg" border="0" height="155" width="265"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><i>yourpassword</i></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">The terminal window is now starting up in the user
  home directory</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 85" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image094.jpg" border="0" height="155" width="265"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">You can now use the PC terminal window the same way
  you us the terminal on the Raspberry itself</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<b><span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span></b>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150915"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: Connect to the Raspberry
file system from your windows system using WinSCP:</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: </span></b><span lang="EN-GB">The
connection can only access the rights of the Raspberry user. So the standard
user “pi” will not have the writing rights for multiple directories. </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;" lang="EN-GB">For full access you have
to use the user “root” (user needs to be enabled since it is disabled in
standard setup, procedure shown later in the tutorial), but enabling this user
for SSH access is opening up a significant security risk, so it is recommended
to use as Raspberry based Samba server for full access to specific directories
(shown later in the tutorial).</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open WinSCP on your computer</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 86" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image095.jpg" border="0" height="177" width="281"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Select: New Site</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Select File protocol: SCP</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Port: </span><span lang="EN-US">22</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Lucida Bright&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150916"><span lang="EN-GB">Setup Samba server</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">To have access to the Raspberry file system
using the PC file explorer (it is needed to run Eclipse Smart Home Designer
your PC) you have to setup a Samba server on the Raspberry first.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: You can also follow the alternative instructions
for a openHAB2 centric installation at: </span><a href="http://docs.openhab.org/installation/linux.html#network-sharing"><span class="Heading9Char"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; color: windowtext; text-decoration: none;" lang="EN-GB">http://docs.openhab.org/installation/linux.html#network-sharing</span></span></a></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 112" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image076.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 91" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image080.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Make sure Raspberry is updated (optional)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo apt-get update</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Download samba server to Raspbery (confirm with
  enter)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo apt-get install samba samba-common-bin</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Enter&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open the samba server configuration file in nano
  editor</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo nano /etc/samba/smb.conf</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Go to the end of the file and add following lines</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">[RaspberryPiDirectories]</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">comment = Your full access to Raspberry Pi
  directories</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">path = /</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">read only = no</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional Change the workgroup name if needed,
  otherwise uncomment and enable WINS support in the section</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"># Windows Internet Name Serving Support Section:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"># WINS Support - Tells the NMBD component of Samba
  to enable its WINS Server</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">#&nbsp;&nbsp; wins support = no</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">wins support = yes</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Exit and save the file</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;ctrl+x&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;y&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Enter&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Check the syntax of the samba configuration file.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Result: there should be no error message(red) in the
  prompt</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">testparm</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Enter&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now you have to restart the services to reload the
  config file</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl restart smbd.service</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl restart nmbd.service</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Make sure that the services are running again
  without errors</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl status smbd.service</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl status nmbd.service</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150917"><span lang="EN-GB">Common samba server commands:</span></a></h3>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl status smbd.service</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl status nmbd.service</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Check if all the services are running</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl restart smbd.service</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl restart nmbd.service </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Restart the samba services</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl stop smbd.service</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl stop nmbd.service</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Manually stop the samba services</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo smbpasswd -d <i>sambausr</i></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">If needed: disable a user for samba</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo smbpasswd -e <i>sambausr</i></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">If you need to enable a user for samba</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150918"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: Generic samba user setup</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> Skip
this section if you only want to use samba for openHAB2</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Create a special user<i> </i></span><i><span lang="EN-US">sambausr</span></i><i><span lang="EN-US"> </span></i><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;for the samba server so you not have to use the root or pi user
  to allow access to the directories on the Raspberry</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo adduser sambausr</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">You have to enter your password</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><i><span lang="EN-US">sambausrpassword</span></i><span lang="EN-GB"> and
  optional information you can just leave empty and finally save with y</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Adding user `sambausr' ...</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Adding new group `sambausr' (1001) ...</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Adding new user `sambausr' (1001) with group `sambausr'
  ...</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Creating home directory `/home/sambausr' ...</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Copying files from `/etc/skel' ...</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Enter new UNIX password:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Retype new UNIX password:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">passwd: password updated successfully</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Changing the user information for sambausr</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Enter the new value, or press ENTER for the default</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Full Name []:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Room Number []:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Work Phone []:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Home Phone []:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Other []:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Is the information correct? </span>[Y/n] y</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Map the user for Samba with</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo smbpasswd -a sambausr</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Enter the password </span><i>sambausrpassword</i></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">New SMB password:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Retype new SMB password:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">Added user sambausr.</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> Instead
of allowing the </span><i><span lang="EN-US">sambausr</span></i><span lang="EN-US">
</span><span lang="EN-GB">to have full access on the Raspbian file system to some
specific folders by applying the </span><span lang="EN-US">chown</span><span lang="EN-GB"> command, you might consider enable the root user and use the root
user to connect to the Raspberry from the file system (see chapter Optional Raspberry
settings and configuration). But be aware that enabling the “root” user is
creating a security risk!</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">

  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">

  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Enter the password </span><i>rootpassword</i></p>

  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 244.45pt;" valign="top" width="326">

  </td>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150919"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional: Mapping Raspbian samba directories
to Windows (IOS and Linux mapping process can be found online):</span></a></h2>

<p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE:</span></b><span lang="EN-GB"> Skip
this section if you only want to use samba for openHAB2</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">One time map the Raspberry folder to a windows drive
  (in this case </span><span lang="EN-US">Z</span><span lang="EN-GB">) enter in the
  CMD Prompt (just put </span><span lang="EN-US">CMD</span><span lang="EN-GB"> in
  the search of Windows 10 to open the command prompt)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">net use Z: \\<i>xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx</i>\RaspberryPiDirectories
  /user:sambausr <i>sambausrpassword </i>/persistent:no</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Persistent map the Raspberry folder to a windows
  drive (in this case </span><span lang="EN-US">Z</span><span lang="EN-GB">) enter
  in the CMD Prompt (just put </span><span lang="EN-US">CMD</span><span lang="EN-GB"> in the search of Windows 10 to open the command prompt)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">net use Z: \\<i>xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx</i>\RaspberryPiDirectories
  /user:sambausr <i>sambausrpassword </i>/persistent:yes</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 239.95pt;" valign="top" width="320">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">You can also create a simple *.bat file for easy
  double clicking.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open the editor by just putting </span><span lang="EN-US">notepad</span><span lang="EN-GB"> in the search of Windows 10</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Enter the line</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Save as </span><i><span lang="EN-US">yourmapping</span></i><span lang="EN-US">.bat</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 252.75pt;" valign="top" width="337">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">net use Z: \\<i>xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx</i>\RaspberryPiDirectories
  /user:sambausr <i>sambausrpassword </i>/persistent:no</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc485150920"><span lang="EN-GB">Chapter 6: Installation of
openHAB2 on Raspberry</span></a></h1>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">This tutorial is only focussing on the
package repository installation of the stable version and only on the add-ons
for the listed hardware. All other installations are described on the
openhab.org site installation for Linux: (</span><a href="http://docs.openhab.org/installation/linux.html#package-repository-installation"><span class="Heading9Char"><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; color: windowtext; text-decoration: none;" lang="EN-GB">http://docs.openhab.org/installation/linux.html#package-repository-installation</span></span></a><span lang="EN-GB">) For the Raspbian you have to go for the “Apt Based Systems” part
of it.</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 218.05pt;" valign="top" width="291">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Open Terminal</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 274.65pt;" valign="top" width="366">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 113" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image076.jpg" alt="Ähnliches Foto" border="0" height="26" width="31"><img id="Picture 92" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image098.jpg" border="0" height="24" width="167"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 218.05pt;" valign="top" width="291">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">First, add the openHAB2 bintray repository key to
  your package manager and allow Apt to use the HTTPS Protocol</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 274.65pt;" valign="top" width="366">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">wget -qO -
  'https://bintray.com/user/downloadSubjectPublicKey?username=openhab' | sudo
  apt-key add -</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo apt-get install apt-transport-https</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 218.05pt;" valign="top" width="291">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">I choose the stable Official (Stable) build</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">The stable builds contain the latest official
  release with tested features.</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 274.65pt;" valign="top" width="366">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">echo 'deb https://dl.bintray.com/openhab/apt-repo2
  stable main' | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/openhab2.list</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 218.05pt;" valign="top" width="291">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Next, resynchronize the package index:</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 274.65pt;" valign="top" width="366">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">sudo apt-get update</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 218.05pt;" valign="top" width="291">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now install openHAB2 with the following command:</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 274.65pt;" valign="top" width="366">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo apt-get install openhab2</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 218.05pt;" valign="top" width="291">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional but recommended: When you choose to install
  an add-on, openHAB2 will download it from the internet on request. If you
  plan on disconnecting your machine from the internet, then you will want to
  also install the add-ons package.</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 274.65pt;" valign="top" width="366">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo apt-get install openhab2-addons</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 218.05pt;" valign="top" width="291">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Since we were installing the stable version, we have
  to manually add the binding WIFILED used for the WiFi LED controller manually
  to the system.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">First you have to change to the add-ons directory.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Than you have to download the latest version of the
  binding directly from the online repository</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: Later, this binding will not be available in
  the PAPER UI GUI under the Add-ons/Bindings tab, but will show up in the
  configuration/bindings tab (note here)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 30" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image099.jpg" border="0" height="138" width="187"></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 274.65pt;" valign="top" width="366">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">cd /usr/share/openhab2/addons</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo
wget
https://openhab.ci.cloudbees.com/job/openHAB2-Bundles/lastSuccessfulBuild/org.openhab.binding%24org.openhab.binding.wifiled/artifact/org.openhab.binding/org.openhab.binding.wifiled/2.1.0-SNAPSHOT/org.openhab.binding.wifiled-2.1.0-SNAPSHOT.jar</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">(but here!)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 28" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image100.jpg" border="0" height="143" width="269"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 218.05pt;" valign="top" width="291">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">If everything went well, you can start openHAB2 and
  register it to be automatically executed at system startup.</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 274.65pt;" valign="top" width="366">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl start openhab2.service</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl status openhab2.service</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl daemon-reload</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">sudo systemctl enable openhab2.service</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-GB"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span>
