  influence the dimming of the WHITE</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; so if you want to set
  both values at the same time, always</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; set color first and than</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; set the dimming of WHITE</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//Changing the color of the item
  HFLPB100ZJ200_Color to RED</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//openHAB2 is requesting the color
  to be set in HSL code (Hue, Saturation, Lightness" or in openHAB terms
  "HSBType" (Hue, Saturation, Brightness)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//To convert RGB code to HSL code
  just go to e.g. http://www.rapidtables.com/convert/color/rgb-to-hsl.htm</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <i>sendCommand</i> (<u>HFLPB100ZJ200_Color</u>,(</span><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);" lang="EN-US">new</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">
  HSBType(</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(42, 0, 255);" lang="EN-US">"0,100,50"</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">)))&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//Dimming the item
  HFLPB100ZJ200_White to 50%</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <i>sendCommand</i> (<u>HFLPB100ZJ200_White</u>,
  </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(125, 125, 125);" lang="EN-US">50</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//Scene number 8 - Button 4 (up
  left) pressed long</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);" lang="EN-US">if</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US"> (<u>ZWaveNode9ZW0884ButtonKeyfobGen5_SceneNumber</u>.state
  == </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(125, 125, 125);" lang="EN-US">8</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">) {</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//NOTE: since setting the color will
  influence the dimming of the WHITE</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; so if you want to set
  both values at the same time, always</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; set color first and than</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; set the dimming of WHITE</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//Changing the color of the item
  HFLPB100ZJ200_Color to GREEN</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//openHAB2 is requesting the color
  to be set in HSL code (Hue, Saturation, Lightness" or in openHAB terms "HSBType"
  (Hue, Saturation, Brightness)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//To convert RGB code to HSL code
  just go to e.g. http://www.rapidtables.com/convert/color/rgb-to-hsl.htm</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <i>sendCommand</i> (<u>HFLPB100ZJ200_Color</u>,(</span><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);" lang="EN-US">new</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">
  HSBType(</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(42, 0, 255);" lang="EN-US">"120,100,50"</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">)))</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">//Dimming
  the item HFLPB100ZJ200_White to 100%</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;">sendCommand</span></i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;"> (<u>HFLPB100ZJ200_White</u>,
  </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(125, 125, 125);">100</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;">)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);">end</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 125.9pt;" valign="top" width="168">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Save the rule file.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">The rule should now be available</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 366.8pt;" valign="top" width="489">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">&lt;crtl+s&gt;</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">Test it by clicking through the buttons
(pressed long and pressed short)<br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150958"><span lang="EN-US">Basic tips for debugging rules</span></a></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150959"><span lang="EN-US">Creating an item the see the value
of a variable of a rule online</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">The standard way of debugging a rule would
be to use a logfile.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">For simple problems you might also be able
to visualize the variables online by creation item with the same type and
posting the value of the variable inside the rule</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">If you are using a variable in your rule initially
  set to </span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">var Number loop_counter = 0</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Create the item </span><span lang="EN-US">Counter_Item</span><span lang="EN-GB"> with the same type:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">In PAPER UI switch to</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-Configuration</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">--Items </span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">And press the blue icon (+)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Enter Name Counter_Item</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Select Typ </span>&lt;Number&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">And confirm the creation by clicking again on the
  blue icon (+)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 174" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image174.jpg" border="0" height="104" width="252"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Counter_Item</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Number&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;(+)&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Result:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">A new item called </span><span lang="EN-US">Counter_Item</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">should be visible in the item tab</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: Since this Item is not linked to a thing it
  will not show up in the </span>&lt;Control&gt; <span lang="EN-GB">Tab to PAPER
  UI.</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 179" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image175.jpg" border="0" height="26" width="306"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now enter a line into your rule to post the value of
  the </span>var<span lang="EN-GB"> to the </span><span lang="EN-US">Counter_Item</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">postUpdate(Counter_Item, loop_counter)</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">To show the value on a dashboard you have to use
  e.g. HABPANEL</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Start HABPANEL</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">http://xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx:8080/HABPANEL/index.html#/</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">and select </span>&lt;Edit dashboards&gt;<span lang="EN-GB"> in the upper right corner</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">then &lt;Add new dashboard&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">enter the name </span>Debug<span lang="EN-GB"> and </span>&lt;OK&gt;</p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 199" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image176.png" border="0" height="80" width="136"><img id="Picture 200" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image177.jpg" border="0" height="55" width="147"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 201" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image178.jpg" border="0" height="82" width="196"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">Debug</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;OK&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now you should have the dashboard </span>&lt;Debug&gt;<span lang="EN-GB"> available in your HABPANEL</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Select the dashboard</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 202" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image179.jpg" border="0" height="129" width="244"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">If you now hover with your mouse right of the
  dashboard name the </span><span lang="EN-US">&lt;Edit <i>Debug</i>&gt; </span><span lang="EN-GB">icon will appear.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Click on it to enter the edit mode.</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 203" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image180.png" border="0" height="76" width="244"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Edit <i>Debug</i>&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">The edit mode is indicated by the two icons </span>&lt;Save&gt;<span lang="EN-GB"> and </span>&lt;Run&gt;</p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 205" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image181.png" border="0" height="43" width="187"></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now you have to </span>&lt;+ Add Widget&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">You have to use the </span>&lt;Dummy&gt;<span lang="EN-GB"> widget to display numbers</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 204" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image182.jpg" border="0" height="126" width="105"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;+ Add Widget&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Dummy&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 276.05pt;" valign="top" width="368">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">The new Widget will appear on your dashboard</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: you can easily change the size of the widget
  by dragging the lower right corner. I will snap to a predefined grid</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 216.65pt;" valign="top" width="289">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 206" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image183.jpg" border="0" height="100" width="114">&nbsp;</p>
  </td>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">To edit the widget you have to click on the 3 dots
  in the upper right corner of the widget and select </span>&lt;Edit&gt;</p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Edit&gt;</p>
  </td>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">In this window you can change the name to </span>Counter
  Item Debug</p>

  <p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span lang="EN-GB">Optional you can change font size, add
  a unit and format or add some icons.</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span lang="EN-GB">Now </span>&lt;Save&gt;<span lang="EN-GB"> the widget.</span></p>
  </td>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Counter_Item&gt;</p>

<b><span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: &quot;Calibri Light&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-US"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span></b>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150960"><span lang="EN-US">Creating a virtual switch on
HABPANEL to use it in a rule</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">This switch might come handy if you are
debugging your rule while physically having no access to the switch. Standing
up and running to the switch might do you some good when it comes down to
fitness but surely is disturbing while developing your rule</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 281.7pt;" valign="top" width="376">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Create the item </span><span lang="EN-US">Dummy_Switch</span><span lang="EN-GB"> with the same type:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">In PAPER UI switch to</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">-Configuration</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">--Items </span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">And press the blue icon (+)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Enter Name Dummy_Switch</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Select Typ </span>&lt;Switch&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">And confirm the creation by clicking again on the
  blue icon (+)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: solid solid solid none; border-color: windowtext windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: 1pt 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 211pt;" valign="top" width="281">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><img id="Picture 231" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image190.jpg" border="0" height="118" width="271"></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">Dummy_Switch</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;Switch&gt;</p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;">&lt;(+)&gt;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 281.7pt;" valign="top" width="376">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Result:</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">A new item called </span><span lang="EN-US">Dummy_Switch</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">should be visible in the item tab</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">NOTE: Since this Item is not linked to a thing it
  will not show up in the </span>&lt;Control&gt; <span lang="EN-GB">Tab to PAPER
  UI.</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 211pt;" valign="top" width="281">

  </td>
 </tr>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now replace the item name of the </span><i>physical_switch</i><span lang="EN-GB"> with the name of the </span><span lang="EN-US">Dummy_Switch</span></p>
  </td>
  <td style="border-style: none solid solid none; border-color: -moz-use-text-color windowtext windowtext -moz-use-text-color; border-width: medium 1pt 1pt medium; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 211pt;" valign="top" width="281">

  </td>
 </tr>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">Now </span>&lt;Save&gt;<span lang="EN-GB"> the
  dashboard and </span>&lt;Run&gt; <span lang="EN-GB">it.</span></p>

  </td>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB">You will now see the </span>Dummy_Switch <span lang="EN-GB">Item be visualized by the </span>Dummy Switch ON/OFF <span lang="EN-GB">widget.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>

<span style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;" lang="EN-US"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc485150961"><span lang="EN-US">Further Rule examples based on
this home automation project:</span></a></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc485150962"><span lang="EN-US">Switching ON/OFF switches based on
luminance reading of the multisensory</span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">The rule is designed to switch on/off the Z-Wave
Node 2: FGS223 Double Switch 2 based on the </span>illumination measured by the
<span lang="EN-US">Z-Wave Node 6: ZW100 MultiSensor 6</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">The trigger value is set to 10 LUX </span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">To prevent von switching on/off if the illumination
is around 10 lumen and e.g. just a cloud is casting a temporarily shadow, there
is a counter included which is measuring multiple times the illumination and
only allows to triggering the switch if there reading is consistently (10
times) above or below the trigger value.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">NOTE: Make sure you have create the item Counter_Item
since it’s used in the rule (see: part “Creating an item the see the value of a
variable of a rule online” in this chapter). </span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">REMARK: This was done as some kind of
coding and configuring HABPANEL exercise. You might get the same result in just
checking the reading in a less frequent period, forget about the counter and
just trigger the switch when the illumination reading is above or below the
trigger value.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">You can also use this Counter_Item to
display some tendency whether your light is about to switch ON/OFF depending on
the value of the Counter_Item on your dashboard. So if you play a little with
the “knob” widget in HABPANEL it might look like this:</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><img id="Picture 243" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image200.jpg" border="0" height="113" width="115">&nbsp;<img id="Picture 244" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image201.jpg" border="0" height="113" width="115">&nbsp;<img id="Picture 245" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image202.jpg" border="0" height="113" width="115">&nbsp;<img id="Picture 246" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image203.jpg" border="0" height="113" width="114"></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">Then you add some other readings of your
multissor, the wattage reading and trigger of your switch, a clock widget and
you have a complete dashboard of your real weather and let it trigger your
outside ligth.</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><img id="Picture 247" src="openHAB2_Raspberry_beginner-s_walkthrough_files/image204.jpg" border="0" height="275" width="510"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="page-break-before: always;" clear="all">
</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">You can just add these lines at the bottom
of your existing rule file or create a new file in the same folder</span></p>

<table class="MsoTableGrid" style="border: medium none ; border-collapse: collapse;" border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="border: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0cm 5.4pt; width: 488.9pt;" valign="top" width="652">

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);" lang="EN-US">var</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US"> Number
  loop_counter = </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(125, 125, 125);" lang="EN-US">0</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">// using the loop_counter to ensure
  that it is</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(63, 127, 95);" lang="EN-US">// 10 times in a row darker/lighter
  before triggering switch</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <i>postUpdate</i>(<u>Counter_Item</u>,

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);" lang="EN-US">else</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US"> {</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);" lang="EN-US">if</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US"> (<u>DoubbleSwitch01_Relais1</u>.state
  == </span><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(0, 0, 192);" lang="EN-US">ON</span></i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">)</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <i>sendCommand</i> (<u>DoubbleSwitch01_Relais1</u>,

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);" lang="EN-US">else</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US"> {</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;" lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(0, 0, 192);">loop_counter</span></i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;"> = </span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(125, 125, 125);">0</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: black;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; line-height: normal;"><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; color: rgb(127, 0, 85);">end</span></b></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">And save the file</span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
